About Medical Care in Orange County

Orange County, Florida is home to 5233 verified medical professionals spanning 33 specialties. The county's healthcare landscape includes specialists in Family Medicine, Internal Medicine, Anesthesiology, Emergency Medicine, Psychiatry, ensuring residents have access to comprehensive medical care.

With doctors practicing in 141 cities across the county, including ORLANDO, WINTER PARK, TAMPA, patients can find quality healthcare close to home. 1553 doctors are also willing to travel, providing additional flexibility for patients with mobility challenges or those in underserved areas.

All doctors listed on EliteMD are verified through the National Provider Identifier (NPI) Registry, ensuring accurate credentials and practice information. Our directory helps patients make informed decisions when choosing a healthcare provider in Orange County.

Frequently Asked Questions

How many doctors are in Orange County, Florida?
EliteMD lists 5233 verified medical professionals across 33 specialties in Orange County, Florida. This includes specialists in Family Medicine, Internal Medicine, Anesthesiology, and more.
What are the top medical specialties in Orange County?
The most represented specialties in Orange County are Family Medicine (513 doctors), Internal Medicine (494 doctors), Anesthesiology (354 doctors), Emergency Medicine (311 doctors), Psychiatry (273 doctors).
Which cities in Orange County have the most doctors?
The cities with the most doctors in Orange County are ORLANDO (2396), WINTER PARK (469), TAMPA (466), GAINESVILLE (306), MAITLAND (226).
How are doctors in Orange County verified?
All doctors on EliteMD are verified through the National Provider Identifier (NPI) Registry, a federal database maintained by the Centers for Medicare & Medicaid Services. Each doctor's credentials, specialty, and practice location are confirmed through official records.
Can I find a specialist who will travel to Orange County?
Yes, many specialists on EliteMD are available to travel. Use the "Will Travel" filter on the search page to find doctors willing to come to Orange County for consultations and procedures.
